            <script>
        (function(cb, seconds) {
        var timer;
        var time = seconds * 1000;
        function refresh() {
            clearTimeout(timer);
            timer = setTimeout(cb, time);
        };
        document.addEventListener("click", refresh);
        document.addEventListener("keypress", refresh);
        document.addEventListener("scroll", refresh);
        refresh();
    })(function() {
        location.href = location.href;
    }, "360");
</script>

                            <h2 class="block-title"><svg aria-hidden="true" height="14" width="14"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="#symbol-folder"></use></svg>Notre dossier sur la Saint-Valentin</h2>
